Valence electrons: 
Highest level ( 1 - 7 ) 
S sublevel and p ( sometimes just S ) 
( highest level S and P ) 
for titanium  ( NO D ) 
in this case your highest level is 4s^2 and your valence electrons are 2
for sulfur its 3s^2 and 3p^4 so its 4 + 2 = 6 
for potassium its 4s^1 so its got 1 valence electron  ^9nzG0dRM
